<userid>116984393329178277814</userid><name>Saul Cruz< /name><Time>1570232805087< /Time><rate>2<//rate>< review>
The leasing staff is very friendly and I think they do their best and there is a capacity issue.

Pros:
The property is very nice, I loved the 2 bedroom units and the amenities (location, the gym , wifi everywhere and heated pool are awesome).

Cons:
Unfortunately the communication between the staff and "future residents" is very poor, it seems to me that we are the ones that need them and not the other way around (which is fine if that's what the market says), however we're not supposed to feel that way.
I had to cancel my morning meetings for a visit to one of their units however the unit was not available for a visit yet which is fine but we were not told about it until we were there.
Also, the waiting at the lobby is terrible, first time we waited around 30 minutes even though we had an appointment (via an agent), second time was fine, third time we got cancelled at the moment promising that they were going to send us an email or call about this unit, never happened.

So we decided to go to El Centro Apartments which is across the street and they seemed more down to Earth.</review>

< Review>
This building is very specific. It's basically a frat house for instagrammers and social influencers. Which is cool, but if you don't fit into that category then it might not be the best place for you. It's hard to get a serious workout in at the gym because people are constantly filming in there. Same goes for all the other amenity spaces. A couple times I looked out my window in the middle of the night to see two people having sex in the hot tub. Hallways reek of weed. For the positives, the location is great. It's right on Hollywood and Vine and there are a lot of food and nightlife options in the area as well as banks and pharmacies, pretty much everything you need. Gym can become a photoshoot set but it still is one of the bigger and better gym's I've seen in apartments.< /Review>

<username>Lydia Abler< /username>< resp>

< Rate>
5</Rate>
<Text>This museum is laden with local natural history. Don't let it's small size fool you! They have exhibits covering everything from the indigenous  tribes to the native animals and plants - both on land and in the bay. There is a touch tank, a fossil crate, a bone index, a wide array of native animals on display (mostly stuffed, although there are live bees in an enclosed hive, as well as a live snake), and a full room dedicated to the Ohlone people where you can learn about their traditions and history. The docents are friendly and knowledgeable, ready to answer any questions you may have. And there's a gift shop!</Text>< time>
1502208425730</time>

<rate>4<//rate>< text>
This is a tiny but mighty museum. When I say tiny I'm not kidding. Unlike the tardis it is way bigger on the outside then the inside. Once again I'm not kidding-the outside grounds -which make a nice non beach pic nic spot-are more extensive then the inside parts. This is however a nicely interactive spot. If you have younger children age five on up this is decent spot for them to learn while playing a bit, but like any museum the older your children are the more they will get out of it. They have some fantastic school programs and the after hours events-astronaut meet and greets, lectures, art openings etc. are very much worth the time. If you an adult just passing through it'll take about 20-30 minutes to go through everything including the whale sculpture and gift shop. If you are with children it can be double that.< /text>

<Gmap_id>0x808f855be50fef27:0x3cab34d72c9a540c<//Gmap_id><Pictures>None< /Pictures>< Text>
This is a storage facility worth checking out. I found this place online and called the toll free number and spoke to Matt. He assisted me with renting a unit for my needs on their website. I got a great web rate for the unit. While we were on the call his computer went down, this resulted in my being charged twice for the deposit, but they were happy to credit my account once I provided proof of the mistake.

All of my questions were asked and there is no real catch to the low prices you see online. You do have to get insurance protection for your valuables and it is an additional cost, but probably worth it in the long run. It's for your protection and theirs. As I was getting of the phone with Matt at the call center, I got a call right away from Charlene, who welcomed me aboard and asked if I had additional questions and offered that I come in to take a look at the unit just to be sure it was what I was looking for.

Today, I went in to take care of the financials before I moved in and met Jerry the manager. He is very cool, calm and patient. He drove me around the cute little golf cart to show me the units and space. Place is very very clean, and even though my unit is upstairs, they have a freight elevator (it is working) and a dolly in case you don't have one available. While waiting to finalize my account the power went down twice (not their fault, men were working on the premises) and Jerry just tugged along and thanked me for my patience.

They have some of the best prices around, would be hard to beat them in such a great location in San Leandro and everyone is very friendly and accommodating and they let you know everything you need to know up front. The space is open every day and even late hours should you need to move stuff in or out after 7pm.

I would recommend them to anyone looking for great rates, fast friendly service and a clean, safe area to store your belongings.<//Text>

< review>
My whole experience with this location and it's staff has been wonderful.  I initially made my reservation online for a 5X10 space, thinking that it would be enough for the stuff that I had.  Once I made my reservation online, I immediately received a phone call from the Site Manager, Jerry.  He was very friendly and provided me with all the information I needed.  We discussed what I was going to be storing and determined that I needed a bigger unit.  We set up a time to meet and I was on my way from San Diego.  I did run into a little bit of a snag, but the reps assisted me and I got my unit.
The facility is clean, associates are professional and friendly, and my unit is easily accessible. I think that the location of this facility is great for me, as I am still in transition to finding a new place to live and my things are centrally located. I feel secure knowing that my personal belongings are protected.  The facility is very secure with two gated entrances, security passcodes needed to get in and out of the facility, an onsite manager, and video surveillance.
I can't reiterate it enough, that the staff at this location is great.  Thank you to Jerry and his team.  I recommend this place highly.</review>
